/* Async Callback Prequal+PASIT ASCI tags */
(function(_w, _d) {
  /**
   * ASI Placement ID:
   * QpTgX2: 728x90
   * UtS5qe: 300x250
   * KBe4qS: 320x50 mWeb
   * yxOz7T: 300x250 mWeb
   * zybvQn: 250x250 mWeb
   *
   **/
  _w['asiTimeout'] = 2000;
  _w['asiDebugTime'] = false;
  _w['asiIsCallback'] = false;
  _w['asiCallback'] = function(e) {
    _w['asiIsCallback'] = true;
    if (_w['asiDebugTime']) {
      var b = new Date().getTime();
      var diff = b - e.reqTime;
      console.log('Callback called - ' + b + ' (+' + diff + 'ms)');
    }
   
    if (typeof _w['asiAdsSetup'] != 'undefined' && _w['asiAdsSetup'].length > 0) {
      if (_w['asiDebugTime']) {
        console.log('Callback called. Number of callback: ', _w['asiAdsSetup'].length);
      }
     
      for(var i=0; i<_w['asiAdsSetup'].length; i++){
        if(typeof _w['asiAdsSetup'][i] == 'function') {
          if (_w['asiDebugTime']) {
            var d = new Date().getTime();
            var setup_diff = d - e.reqTime;
            console.log('Setup function ' + (i+1) + ' called - ' + d + ' (+' + setup_diff + 'ms)');
          }
         
          _w['asiAdsSetup'][i]();
        }
      }
    }
  };

  _w['asiPlacementIds'] = isMobile ? ['zybvQn', 'KBe4qS', 'yxOz7T'] : ['QpTgX2', 'UtS5qe'];

  for(var x in asiPlacementIds) { _w['ASPQ_' + asiPlacementIds[x]] = ''; }

  var cb = new Date().getTime();
  var src = "//pq-direct.revsci.net/pql?placementIdList=" + asiPlacementIds.join(',') + "&cb=" + cb;
  var e = _d.createElement("script");
  var s = _d.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
  e.async = true;
  e.onload = function () { // PASIT
    if (_w['asiDebugTime']) {
      var b = new Date().getTime();
      var diff = b - this.reqTime;
      console.log('Response received - ' + b + ' (+' + diff + 'ms)');
    }

    if (!_w['asiIsCallback']) {
      if (typeof asiPlacements != "undefined") {
        for (var asiPlId in asiPlacements) {
          _w["ASPQ_" + asiPlId] = "";
          if (typeof asiPlacements[asiPlId] != "undefined" && typeof asiPlacements[asiPlId].default != "undefined") {
            for(var key in asiPlacements[asiPlId].data) {
              // ASPQ variable value
              _w["ASPQ_" + asiPlId] += "PQ_" + asiPlId + "_" + key;
            }
          }
        }
      }

      _w['asiCallback'](e);
    }
  };

  var asiFallback = function() {
    if (!asiPqTag) {
      // continue e.onload when debug is on
      if (!_w['asiDebugTime']) {
        e.onload = null;
      }
    
      asiPlacements = null;
      _w['asiCallback'](e);
    }
  };
 e.onerror = asiFallback;
  e.src = src;
  if (_w['asiDebugTime']) {
    e.reqTime = new Date().getTime();
  }
  s.parentNode.insertBefore(e, s);

  if (typeof _w['asiAdsSetup'] != 'undefined' && _w['asiAdsSetup'].length > 0) {
    setTimeout(asiFallback, asiTimeout);
  }
  if (_w['asiDebugTime']) {
    console.log('Send PQL Request - ', e.reqTime);
  }
})(window, document);

/* End of Async Callback Prequal+PASIT ASCI tags */
